Neuton ExtraLight Regular (Neuton-ExtraLight.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Neuton-ExtraLight', Everything looks good.

Pass

Neuton ExtraLight Regular (Neuton-ExtraLight.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Neuton' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraLight' = NID 1 'Neuton ExtraLight'.

Pass

Neuton Light Regular (Neuton-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Neuton' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Neuton Light'.

Neuton Italic (Neuton-Italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Neuton-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.

NID 6 is 'Neuton-Italic', Everything looks good.

Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. Neuton Bold (Neuton-Bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Neuton-Bold', Everything looks good.

Neuton ExtraBold Regular (Neuton-ExtraBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Neuton' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraBold' = NID 1 'Neuton ExtraBold'.
